0                                  19302              *
                                   19303              *  Set up account and scanner fields.
                                   19304              *
                                   19305              *  We set up to scan from a buffer different from
                                   19306              *  WYLBURS command buffer.  We blank out certain WYLBUR
                                   19307              *  options so that they are not passed to JES.  For
                                   19308              *  example all the 'collect options' are blanked so
                                   19309              *  that JES does not have to ignore options that it knows
                                   19310              *  nothing about.  The options are blanked in the JES buffer
                                   19311              *  and not in the WYLBUR buffer.
                                   19312              *
                                   19313              *  ON ENTRY:
                                   19314              *        R1,R0 - Command loc, len
                                   19315              *        R6 = JWA pointer
                                   19316              *
                                   19317              *

0                                  29639              
                                   29640                                                                                   
                                   29641                The JESCOM routine builds a pcw in the JWA and then issues         
                                   29642                an suzan call to send whatever is in the HCB to JES.               
                                   29643                This routine also waits for JES if necessary.                      
                                   29644                                                                                   
                                   29645                On exit:                                                           
                                   29646                    r15 and condition code is zero if there is data waiting        
                                   29647                    to be processed in the suzan buffer and non-zero if            
                                   29648                    something went wrong (e.g., JES closing the path).             
                                   29649

0                                  29886              
                                   29887                                                                                   
                                   29888                PATHSTAT -- Routine to check the status of JES suzan path.         
                                   29889                                                                                   
                                   29890                  On entry:                                                        
                                   29891                    R1 - HCMRSC ptr                                                
                                   29892                                                                                   
                                   29893                  On exit, R15 (and cc):                                           
                                   29894                   -4 - no data in buffer                                          
                                   29895                    0 - data in buffer                                             
                                   29896                    4 - path just closed (and has been re-opened)                  
                                   29897                    8 - path is closed (waiting for it to be opened)               
                                   29898
